\isamarkupsubsection{Syntax of the Language%

{\isafolddocument}%

\isakeywordONE{type{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}synonym}\isamarkupfalse%
\ link\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ nat\isanewline
\isakeywordONE{type{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}synonym}\isamarkupfalse%
\ links\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}link\ list{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
We use natural numbers as link identifiers.
A value of type \isa{\isatconst{link}} represents a single link name,
and a value of type \isa{\isatconst{links}} represents a finite list of such names.
Links are handled using de Bruijn indices: the number \isa{{\isadigit{0}}} refers to the
innermost bound link, \isa{{\isadigit{1}}} to the next one, and so on.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{datatype}\isamarkupfalse%
\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ Zero\isanewline
\ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ Atom\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ p{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ links\isanewline
\ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ Fusion\ link\ link\isanewline
\ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ Mol\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ Nu\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isakeywordTWO{and}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ Graph\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ App\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}\isakeywordTWO{infixl}\ {\isacartoucheopen}{\isasymcdot}{\isacartoucheclose}\ {\isadigit{2}}{\isadigit{0}}{\isadigit{0}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ Case\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}links\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ list{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isakeywordTWO{and}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ p\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ GConstr\ string\isanewline
\ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ GVar\ nat\isanewline
\ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ GAbs\ links\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
The syntax of HyperLMNtal graphs, expressions, and atomic patterns is
given by mutually recursive datatypes.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Free links of graphs.
The constructor Nu binds the link index 0 in its subgraph,
and all other free links are shifted down by one.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{primrec}\isamarkupfalse%

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Some helper functions for building a graph.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%

\isatagdocument
%
\isamarkupsubsection{Variable Lift and Graph Substitution%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%
%
\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
The lifting operation \isa{\isafree{lift}\ \isafree{t}\ \isafree{k}} shifts free de Bruijn indices
stored in \isa{\isaconst{GVar}} that are greater than by 1.
When we go under an \isa{\isaconst{GAbs}} binder, we increase the cutoff to \isa{\isafree{k}\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}}.
Graph-level binders \isa{\isaconst{Nu}} bind links, not expression variables,
so they do not affect the cutoff for lifting expression variables.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{primrec}\isamarkupfalse%
\ lift\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}nat\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isakeywordTWO{and}\ lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}atom\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}nat\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ p\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ p{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isakeywordTWO{and}\ lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}nat\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isakeywordTWO{where}\isanewline
\ \ \isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift\ k\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}Graph\ g{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Graph\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ k\ g{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift\ k\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}App\ e{\isadigit{1}}\ e{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ App\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift\ k\ e{\isadigit{1}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift\ k\ e{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift\ k\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}Case\ e\ {\isasymGamma}\ T\ e{\isadigit{1}}\ e{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Case\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift\ k\ e{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymGamma}\ T\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}k\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ length\ {\isasymGamma}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ e{\isadigit{1}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift\ k\ e{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isanewline
\ \ \isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}atom\ k\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}GConstr\ s{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ GConstr\ s{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}atom\ k\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}GVar\ i{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}if\ i\ {\isacharless}{\kern0pt}\ k\ then\ GVar\ i\ else\ GVar\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}i\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}atom\ k\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}GAbs\ {\isasymtau}\ xs\ e{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ GAbs\ {\isasymtau}\ xs\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}k\ {\isacharplus}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ e{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline

\ \ \isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ k\ Zero\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Zero{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline

{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ k\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}Mol\ g{\isadigit{1}}\ g{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Mol\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ k\ g{\isadigit{1}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ k\ g{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ k\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}Nu\ g{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Nu\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ k\ g{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Capture-avoiding substitution \isa{\isafree{e{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}}\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}\isafree{e}\ {\isacharslash}{\kern0pt}\ \isafree{i}{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}} on expressions, atoms, and graphs.
This is a structural skeleton; the behavior on variable occurrences (GVar)
must be decided to make this a real substitution.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{primrec}\isamarkupfalse%
\ subst\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}nat\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ links\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isakeywordTWO{and}\ subst{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}graph\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}nat\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ links\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isakeywordTWO{and}\ subst{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}p\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}nat\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ links\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ p\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ links\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ graph{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isakeywordTWO{where}\isanewline

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Values are exactly abstractions and base-type literals.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{primrec}\isamarkupfalse%
\ is{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}atom{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}val\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ p\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ bool{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \isakeywordTWO{where}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}is{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}atom{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}val\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}GConstr\ s{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ True{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}is{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}atom{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}val\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}GAbs\ xs\ ty\ e{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ True{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}is{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}atom{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}val\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}GVar\ i{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ False{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Values are exactly abstractions and base-type literals.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Values are exactly abstractions and base-type literals.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{primrec}\isamarkupfalse%
\ is{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}val\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}ty\ exp\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ bool{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \isakeywordTWO{where}\isanewline

\isatagdocument
%
\isamarkupsubsection{Type System%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%
%
\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
We first define environments and then define typing relations.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Environments%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Environments are represented as lists, where the head corresponds to the
most recently inserted binding (de Bruijn-style contexts).%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{type{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}synonym}\isamarkupfalse%
\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ env\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ list{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
\isa{\isafree{insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at}\ \isafree{xs}\ \isafree{j}\ \isafree{x}} inserts element x at position j in xs.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{fun}\isamarkupfalse%
\ insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ env\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ nat\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a\ env{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \isakeywordTWO{where}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ xs\ \ \ \ \ \ \ {\isadigit{0}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ x\ {\isacharhash}{\kern0pt}\ xs{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}Suc\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}x{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}y\ {\isacharhash}{\kern0pt}\ ys{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}Suc\ n{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ x\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ y\ {\isacharhash}{\kern0pt}\ insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ ys\ n\ x{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Types and Typing Rules%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Simple types:

%
\begin{itemize}%
\item \isa{TBase\ n\ xs} : base type identified by \isa{n} with free links \isa{xs}

\item \isa{TArrow\ ty{\isadigit{1}}\ ty{\isadigit{2}}\ xs} : function type \isa{ty{\isadigit{1}}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ ty{\isadigit{2}}} with free links \isa{xs}.

\item \isa{TLI\ tys\ ty\ xs} : linear implication type with hided links \isa{xs}.%
\end{itemize}%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{datatype}\isamarkupfalse%
\ type\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ TBase\ nat\ links\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ TArrow\ type\ type\ links\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ TLI\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}type\ multiset{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ nat\ links\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}link\ fset{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Typing environments map de Bruijn indices to (links, type) pairs.
The head is the most recently bound variable.
Normally: var -> var
This: var, links -> var, links.
Thus: links -> type.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{type{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}synonym}\isamarkupfalse%
\ tyenv\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}links\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ type{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ list{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Right-hand side of a production rule.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{type{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}synonym}\isamarkupfalse%
\ prodrule{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}RHS\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}nat\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}string\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ links{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}link\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ link{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ list\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ type\ list{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Whole production rule: left-hand side tag / links and RHS.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{type{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}synonym}\isamarkupfalse%
\ prodrule\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}nat\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ links{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ prodrule{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}RHS{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
A set of the free links of a type.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{primrec}\isamarkupfalse%
\ FLty\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}type\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ link\ set{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \isakeywordTWO{where}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}FLty\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}TBase\ i\ xs{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ set\ xs{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}FLty\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}TArrow\ ty{\isadigit{1}}\ ty{\isadigit{2}}\ xs{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ set\ xs{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}FLty\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}TLI\ tys\ a\ xs\ ys{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ fset\ ys{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
A set of the all the free links of a type.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{primrec}\isamarkupfalse%
\ ALty\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}type\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ link\ set{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \isakeywordTWO{where}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}ALty\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}TBase\ i\ xs{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ set\ xs{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}ALty\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}TArrow\ ty{\isadigit{1}}\ ty{\isadigit{2}}\ xs{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ set\ xs{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}ALty\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}TLI\ tys\ a\ xs\ ys{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymUnion}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}set{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}mset\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}image{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}mset\ ALty\ tys{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymunion}\ set\ xs\ {\isasymunion}\ fset\ ys{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isanewline
\isanewline
\isanewline
\isakeywordONE{lemma}\isamarkupfalse%
\ FLty{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}subset{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}ALty{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}FLty\ ty\ {\isasymsubseteq}\ ALty\ ty{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
%
\isadelimproof
%
\endisadelimproof

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Call-by-value small-step relation on expressions.
- Perform beta only when the argument graph is already a value.
- Case on a value graph that matches the pattern graph.
- Case on a non-graph value (falls through to the else branch).
- Evaluate the function part first (left-to-right).
- Then evaluate the argument, once the function is a value.
No reduction happens inside abstractions.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{inductive}\isamarkupfalse%
\ cbv{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}ty\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}type\ exp\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ prodrule\ list\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ type\ exp\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ bool{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Inserting y at the front and then U at position Suc i is the same as
first inserting U at position i and then y at the front.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{lemma}\isamarkupfalse%
\ shift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}commute{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ {\isachardoublequoteopen}insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ xs\ i\ y{\isadigit{1}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{0}}\ y{\isadigit{2}}\isanewline
\ \ \ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ xs\ {\isadigit{0}}\ y{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}Suc\ i{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ y{\isadigit{1}}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
%
\isadelimproof
%
\endisadelimproof

\isatagdocument
%
\isamarkupsection{Soundness%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\isamarkupsubsection{Substitution Lemma%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%
%
\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
We first show that lifting preserves well-typedness.
The lifting operation shifts free variable indices in an expression.
This lemma shows that lifting preserves typing:
if e is well-typed in environment $\Gamma$,
then lifting e by i yields a well-typed term in the environment
extended by inserting $\tau$' at position i.
This property is crucial for the substitution lemma,
particularly under the abstraction case.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{lemma}\isamarkupfalse%
\ lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}type{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeywordTWO{assumes}\ T{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isasymGamma}\ {\isasymturnstile}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ e\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ ty{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \isakeywordTWO{and}\ LE{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}i\ {\isasymle}\ length\ {\isasymGamma}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeywordTWO{shows}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}insert{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}at\ {\isasymGamma}\ i\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}ys{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ ty{\isadigit{2}}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymturnstile}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}lift\ i\ e{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ ty{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
%

\endisadelimproof

\isatagdocument
%
\isamarkupsubsection{Subject Reduction%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%
%
\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Subject reduction:
  If a term e reduces to e' by a call-by-value step,
  and e is well-typed,
  then e' is also well-typed with the same type.
  This ensures that evaluation preserves typing.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{lemma}\isamarkupfalse%
\ weakening{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}right{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeywordTWO{assumes}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isasymGamma}\ {\isasymturnstile}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ e\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymtau}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeywordTWO{shows}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isasymGamma}{\isacharat}{\kern0pt}{\isasymGamma}{\isadigit{2}}\ {\isasymturnstile}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ e\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymtau}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
%
\isadelimproof
%
\endisadelimproof

\isadelimproof

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Subject reduction:
  If a term e reduces to e' by a call-by-value step,
  and e is well-typed,
  then e' is also well-typed with the same type.
  This ensures that evaluation preserves typing.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{lemma}\isamarkupfalse%
\ subject{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}reduction{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline

\ \ \ \ \ \ \isakeywordTWO{and}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}e\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ e{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeywordTWO{shows}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isasymGamma}\ {\isasymturnstile}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ e{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymtau}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Multi-step subject reduction:
  If e reduces to e' in zero or more steps,
  then e' has the same type as e.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{corollary}\isamarkupfalse%

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Progress: a simpler corollary.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%

\isatagdocument
%
\isamarkupsubsection{Soundness%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%
%
\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Type soundness theorem:
  If a closed term is well-typed and reduces (in zero or more steps)
  to some term e', then e' is either a value or can take a further step.
  This combines subject reduction and progress to establish
  the standard type soundness property of the language.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isakeywordONE{theorem}\isamarkupfalse%
\ type{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}soundness{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeywordTWO{assumes}\ WT{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymturnstile}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ e\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymtau}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \isakeywordTWO{and}\ STEPS{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}e\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ e{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeywordTWO{shows}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}is{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}val\ e{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymor}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isasymexists}u{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ e{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}{\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ u{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
%
\isadelimproof
%
\endisadelimproof
%
\isatagproof

\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymturnstile}{\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}P{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ e{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymtau}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \isakeywordONE{using}\isamarkupfalse%
\ STEPS\ WT\ subject{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}reduction{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ \isakeywordONE{by}\isamarkupfalse%
\ blast\isanewline

\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}thesis\ \isakeywordONE{using}\isamarkupfalse%
